It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_CHANNEL = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.\n    PER_TOKEN = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per group. Python code selects `W4A8_MXFP4_INT8` from `QuantAlgo`\n2. `QuantMode.from_quant_algo()` creates the corresponding `QuantMode`\n3.
